### Probability Mass Function

![Graph with seats probability mass function not yet produced](average-seats-pmf-movimento5stelleni.png "Seats Probability Mass Function")

The following table shows the probability mass function per seat for the [poll average](average.html) for Movimento 5 Stelle (NI).

| Number of Seats | Probability | Accumulated | Special Marks |
|:---------------:|:-----------:|:-----------:|:-------------:|
| 10 | 0.2% | 100% |  |
| 11 | 2% | 99.8% |  |
| 12 | 11% | 98% |  |
| 13 | 23% | 87% |  |
| 14 | 31% | 65% | Median |
| 15 | 22% | 34% |  |
| 16 | 10% | 11% |  |
| 17 | 1.4% | 2% | Last Result |
| 18 | 0.1% | 0.1% |  |
| 19 | 0% | 0% |  |
